    <aside id="interscroller_ad" class="interscroller_ad visible-xs center mobile-interscroller " style="width:300px"></aside>
    <script>
        var mps = mps || {};
        mps._queue = mps._queue || {};
        mps._queue.gptloaded = mps._queue.gptloaded || [];
        mps._queue.adload = mps._queue.adload || [];

        mps._queue.gptloaded.push(function() {
            if (mps.getResponsiveSet() =='0') { //MOBILE
                mps.insertAd('#interscroller_ad','interscroller');
            }
        });
        mps._queue.adload.push(function(eo) {
            if (eo._mps._slot === 'interscroller' && eo.isEmpty) {
                document.querySelector('.mobile-interscroller').classList.add('isEmpty');
            }
        });
    </script>

<section id="audience_reviews" class="panel panel-rt panel-box" data-qa="audience-reviews">
    <h2 class="panel-heading">Audience Reviews for <em>Incredibles 2</em></h2>
    
        
        <div class="sr-only js-clamp-live-region" aria-live="polite"></div>
        <ul class="mop-audience-reviews__reviews-wrap clearfix">
            
            
            
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-left cl" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Aug 12, 2020</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">Doesn&#39;t hold a candle to the original Incredibles, and it&#39;s like... really on the nose, but Incredibles 2 is still a good time.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/861960467">
                            
                                <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-default"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/861960467">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Gimly M</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-right cr" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__half "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">May 03, 2019</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">Pixar continues sequelizing their hits with Incredibles 2, a fun and entertaining animated superhero film.  When tech mogul Winston Deavor sees the superhero family The Incredibles saving the city he makes them an offer to partner with them and use his resources to help them improve their public image and get the ban on superheroes repealed.  The animation is really crisp and colorful, and features a host of new superheroes with interesting character designs.  However, the plot is rather formulaic and predictable, but not entirely in a bad way.  Also, the comedy can be a little broad and slapstickly, yet it still delivers a lot of laughs and there are some clever bits of satire.  And, Michael Giacchino provides a pretty good score that compliments the tone and aesthetic of the film.  Ambitious and action-packed, Incredibles 2 is a worthy sequel to one of Pixar&#39;s landmark films.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/906395584">
                            
                                <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-default"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/906395584">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Dann M</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-left cl" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Feb 17, 2019</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">I was happy to see The Incredibles return and for the better part is just as fun as the first film. The problem here is the timing and when the first strolled into cinemas in the early 00&#39;s it was a breath of fresh air, but now this is a very standard comic book movie storyline. It is interesting the story continues exactly where the first film ended, the voice acting has aged as it should have, but this is not explained with the timing of the story. The sequel could have focused on the extended time lost between movies. This doesn&#39;t deduct from the overall score, it&#39;s just my opinion. The issue here is relevance and in the market place, The Incredibles don&#39;t stand out from the pact. This made a lot of money and that is no shock as the original was successful, but didn&#39;t set the world on fire. The original film made a dent at home and that&#39;s where I caught the film and loved it from the first screening. This sequel attempts to capture lightening twice and it struggles to maintain the strength of the first film. The film does hit a point in the story where it gets really good and I feel the shift on Elastigirl is forced in the current climate. The sequel might not be the equivalent of the first, but it is still a lot of fun. 16/02/2019.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/909990449">
                            
                                <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-default"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/909990449">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Brendan N</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-right cr" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Dec 11, 2018</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">Bird looses the plot a bit (he&#39;s always been a little too comfortable with elitism) but the action sequences are even better than they were in the first once.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/790680964">
                            
                                <img class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-avatar" src="https://graph.facebook.com/v3.3/20312798/picture"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/790680964">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Alec B</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
        </ul>
        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__view-all clearfix">
